<p><b>Mats Julian Hummels</b> (<small>German pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Standard_German" title="Help:IPA/Standard German">[mats hmls]</a></span>; born 16 December 1988) is a German professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Centre_back" class="mw-redirect" title="Centre back">centre back</a> for <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany national team</a>.
</p><p>He came through the <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> youth academy before joining <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> on loan in January 2008 and officially signing for Dortmund in February 2009 for €4 million. His honours at the club include two league titles and finishing as runner up in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League">2012–13 UEFA Champions League</a>. In May 2016, Hummels signed a contract with former side Bayern, which took effect on 1 July 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hummels has been a full international since 2010, earning over 70 caps until date and representing Germany at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a>, <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>, <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a> and <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Bayern_Munich:_Youth.2C_and_2006.E2.80.932008"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Bayern_Munich:_Youth,_and_2006–2008">Bayern Munich: Youth, and 2006–2008</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Bayern Munich: Youth, and 2006–2008">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Hummels is a product of <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Bayern_Munich_Junior_Team" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayern Munich Junior Team">youth academy</a>, first entering the club as a six-year-old. He signed his first professional contract on 19 December 2006, until 2010. On 19 May 2007, in <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_Bundesliga" title="2006–07 Bundesliga">the season</a>'s final match, he played his first <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> match with the first team in a 5–2 home routing of <a href="/wiki/1._FSV_Mainz_05" title="1. FSV Mainz 05">1. FSV Mainz 05</a>. He also played for the <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich_II" title="FC Bayern Munich II">reserve team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He played in one match during the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_Regionalliga" title="2005–06 Regionalliga">2005–06 season</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-2005–06_season_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2005–06_season-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> 31 matches during the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_Regionalliga" title="2006–07 Regionalliga">2006–07 season</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> and 10 matches during the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Regionalliga" title="2007–08 Regionalliga">2007–08 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Borussia_Dortmund:_2008.E2.80.932016"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Borussia_Dortmund:_2008–2016">Borussia Dortmund: 2008–2016</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Borussia Dortmund: 2008–2016">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg/220px-Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg/330px-Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg/440px-Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3008" data-file-height="2000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Championship_celebration_Borussia_Dortmund_2011.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Borussia Dortmund players <i>(From Left to Right: <a href="/wiki/Marco_Stiepermann" title="Marco Stiepermann">Marco Stiepermann</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marcel_Schmelzer" title="Marcel Schmelzer">Marcel Schmelzer</a>, Mats Hummels and <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Gro%C3%9Fkreutz" title="Kevin Großkreutz">Kevin Großkreutz</a>)</i> celebrate winning the Bundesliga in <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Bundesliga" title="2010–11 Bundesliga">2011</a></div></div></div>
<p>In January 2008, Hummels joined <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>, initially on loan. He finished the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Borussia_Dortmund_season" title="2007–08 Borussia Dortmund season">2007–08 season</a> with 16 matches played.<sup id="cite_ref-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mats_Hummels_»_Club_matches-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> During his <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Bundesliga" title="2008–09 Bundesliga">first full season</a>, he quickly established himself as first-choice, as he often partnered newly signed <a href="/wiki/Neven_Suboti%C4%87" title="Neven Suboti">Neven Suboti</a>, but also missed a great part of its final months due to injury. In February 2009, he was fully signed to the club<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> for a fee of €4 million.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Borussia_Dortmund_season" title="2008–09 Borussia Dortmund season">2008–09 season</a> with a goal in 14 matches played.<sup id="cite_ref-2008–09_season_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2008–09_season-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Borussia_Dortmund_season" title="2009–10 Borussia Dortmund season">following season</a>, Hummels scored five goals in 33 matches played.<sup id="cite_ref-2009–10_season_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2009–10_season-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg/150px-Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg" decoding="async" width="150" height="247" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg/225px-Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg/300px-Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg 2x" data-file-width="967" data-file-height="1591" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mats_Hummels_2013.jpeg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hummels in action for <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Borussia_Dortmund_season" title="2010–11 Borussia Dortmund season">2010–11 season</a> brought increased success for Hummels. He was the regular first-choice centre back, again paired with Suboti. The duo helped Dortmund to the best defensive record in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Bundesliga" title="2010–11 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a>, as the team won the <a href="/wiki/List_of_German_football_champions" title="List of German football champions">league title</a>. Hummels' performances that season displayed great quality in <a href="/wiki/Sliding_tackle" title="Sliding tackle">tackling</a>, positioning, passing and composure.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He has attracted praise from pundits and coaches alike, and he is considered one of the best defenders in the Bundesliga, and in Europe. Hummels finished the 2010–11 season with six goals in 42 matches played.<sup id="cite_ref-2010–11_season_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2010–11_season-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hummels won the Bundesliga for a second time in <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Bundesliga" title="2011–12 Bundesliga">2011–12</a> as Dortmund set a Bundesliga record with the most points in a Bundesliga season with 81 points. Hummels scored a goal in Dortmund's 5–2 win against Bayern in the <a href="/wiki/2012_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2012 DFB-Pokal Final">2012 DFB-Pokal Final</a> as the team completed the league and cup <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)" title="Double (association football)">double</a>. On 3 June 2012, Hummels signed a new contract that will keep him at Dortmund until the summer of 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 25 May 2013, Hummels was in the Borussia Dortmund line-up that was defeated 2–1 by Bayern Munich at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2013 UEFA Champions League Final">2013 UEFA Champions League Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 July 2013, Hummels was in the Borussia Dortmund line-up that won 4–2 against Bayern Munich at BVB's <a href="/wiki/Signal_Iduna_Park" class="mw-redirect" title="Signal Iduna Park">Signal Iduna Park</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dortmund" title="Dortmund">Dortmund</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/2013_DFL-Supercup" title="2013 DFL-Supercup">2013 DFL-Supercup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hummels finished his Borussia Dortmund career with two goals in 32 matches played in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Borussia_Dortmund_season" title="2014–15 Borussia Dortmund season">2014–15 season</a><sup id="cite_ref-2014–15_season_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2014–15_season-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and three goals in 50 matches played during the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Borussia_Dortmund_season" title="2015–16 Borussia Dortmund season">2015–16 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2015–16_season_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2015–16_season-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Bayern_Munich">Return to Bayern Munich</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Return to Bayern Munich">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2016–17 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 10 May 2016, it was confirmed that Hummels would re-join Bayern Munich from 1 July 2016, signing a five-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He made his 2016 debut for Bayern on 14 August 2016 in the <a href="/wiki/2016_DFL-Supercup" title="2016 DFL-Supercup">German Super Cup</a> final, against his old team and winning 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-Mats_Hummels_eyes_improvement_after_Bayern_debut_at_Dortmund_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mats_Hummels_eyes_improvement_after_Bayern_debut_at_Dortmund-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> On 20 August, Hummels scored his first goal for the club in a 5–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Carl_Zeiss_Jena" title="FC Carl Zeiss Jena">Carl Zeiss Jena</a> during the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_DFB-Pokal" title="2016–17 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> match.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 26 November, Hummels scored his first league goal for the club in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 24 September, Hummels suffered knee injury in his right knee just before half time and was subbed off in a 1–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He made his comeback as a substitute in the second half in a 1–0 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> on 29 September.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 11 March 2017, Hummels made a world class goal-saving tackle on <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Branimir_Hrgota" title="Branimir Hrgota">Branimir Hrgota</a> by making an amazing run towards him and denied him to score from a clear chance.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> On 9 April, Hummels missed the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> quarter-final first leg against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> after sustaining an ankle injury in training.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> On 19 April, he did not fully recover from the injury and had to play the second leg against Real Madrid as defender <a href="/wiki/Javi_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="Javi Martínez">Javi Martínez</a> was shown red card in the first leg and there was no more backup player in centre-back position, but the match ended 4–2 defeat for his side as they got knocked out from the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> On 26 April, Hummels scored a goal against his former club Borussia Dortmund in a 2–3 loss in the DFB-Pokal semi-final.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He finished the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2016–17 FC Bayern Munich season">2016–17 season</a> with three goals and two assists in his forty-one matches.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Hummels finished the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2016–17 FC Bayern Munich season">2016–17 season</a> with three goals in 42 matches played.<sup id="cite_ref-Mats_Hummels_eyes_improvement_after_Bayern_debut_at_Dortmund_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mats_Hummels_eyes_improvement_after_Bayern_debut_at_Dortmund-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2016–17_season_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2016–17_season-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2017–18 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg/220px-Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="252" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg/330px-Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg/440px-Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2065" data-file-height="2370" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mats_Hummels_Training_2018-05-08_FC_Bayern_Muenchen-3.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hummels with <a href="/wiki/Bayern_Munich" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a></div></div></div>
<p>On 5 August 2017, Hummels started the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2017–18 FC Bayern Munich season">season</a> in fashion by defeating Borussia Dortmund to win the <a href="/wiki/2017_DFL-Supercup" title="2017 DFL-Supercup">DFL-Supercup</a> in the penalty-shootout as the match ended 2–2 after extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-2017_German_Super_Cup_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017_German_Super_Cup-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal of the season in a 5–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Chemnitzer_FC" title="Chemnitzer FC">Chemnitzer FC</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_DFB-Pokal" title="2017–18 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> on 12 August.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 1 October, Hummels scored a goal in a 2–2 draw over <a href="/wiki/Hertha_BSC" title="Hertha BSC">Hertha BSC</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On 18 October, he scored his first <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> goal for the club in a 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Hummels sustained an adductor injury at Bayern's training camp in <a href="/wiki/Doha" title="Doha">Doha</a> during the winter break which forced him to miss the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Bundesliga" title="2017–18 Bundesliga">league</a> match against Bayer Leverkusen.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> On 2 February, Hummels played his first match of the year after recovering from the injury in a 2–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/1._FSV_Mainz_05" title="1. FSV Mainz 05">Mainz 05</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> On 31 March, he made his 50th league appearance for Bayern Munich in a 6–0 victory over Borussia Dortmund.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> On 28 April, Hummels captained his side for the first time in a 4–1 victory over Eintracht Frankfurt.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He finished the season with scoring three goals and provided one assist in his forty appearances.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Hummels finished the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2017–18 FC Bayern Munich season">2017–18 season</a> with three goals in 41 matches played.<sup id="cite_ref-2017_German_Super_Cup_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017_German_Super_Cup-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2017–18_season_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2017–18_season-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2018–19 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Hummels started the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2018–19 FC Bayern Munich season">2018–19 season</a> by starting in the <a href="/wiki/2018_DFL-Supercup" title="2018 DFL-Supercup">German Super Cup</a>, which Bayern won 5–0.<sup id="cite_ref-FCB_gewinnt_Supercup_-_Lewandowski_macht_den_Unterschied_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FCB_gewinnt_Supercup_-_Lewandowski_macht_den_Unterschied-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hummels had a difficult spell midway through the season as he lost his starting place for several matches. Hummels was criticized for his comments after the 3–2 loss against Dortmund on 10 November 2018. Hummels blamed his poor performance on him being sick. Hummels said he had blurred vision before the match but he still decided to play the match. Hummels had to be substituted in the second half because of his poor performance.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 18 May 2019, Hummels won his fifth Bundesliga title as Bayern finished two points above Dortmund with 78 points. A week later, Hummels won his second <a href="/wiki/DFB-Pokal" title="DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> as Bayern defeated <a href="/wiki/RB_Leipzig" title="RB Leipzig">RB Leipzig</a> 3–0 in the <a href="/wiki/2019_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2019 DFB-Pokal Final">2019 DFB-Pokal Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hummels finished the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2018–19 FC Bayern Munich season">2018–19 season</a> with two goals in 33 matches played.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Dortmund">Return to Dortmund</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Return to Dortmund">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2019–20 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 19 June 2019, Bayern Munich came to an agreement with Borussia Dortmund that would see the 30-year-old rejoin his former club, for a fee of €37 million (£33 million).<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> He finished his time in Bavaria with 8 goals in 116 appearances. Within those three seasons, he won all three Bundesliga campaigns as well as the <a href="/wiki/DFB-Pokal" title="DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> and three <a href="/wiki/DFL-Supercup" title="DFL-Supercup">DFL-Supercups</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mats_Hummels,_Germany_national_football_team_(03).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Mats_Hummels%2C_Germany_national_football_team_%2803%29.jpg/220px-Mats_Hummels%2C_Germany_national_football_team_%2803%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Mats_Hummels%2C_Germany_national_football_team_%2803%29.jpg/330px-Mats_Hummels%2C_Germany_national_football_team_%2803%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Mats_Hummels%2C_Germany_national_football_team_%2803%29.jpg/440px-Mats_Hummels%2C_Germany_national_football_team_%2803%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="1800" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mats_Hummels,_Germany_national_football_team_(03).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Hummels playing for <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a></div></div></div>
<p>Hummels was called by the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_under-21_football_team" title="Germany national under-21 football team">German under-21 national team</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-21_Championship" title="2009 UEFA European Under-21 Championship">2009 UEFA European Under-21 Championship</a>; after getting only minimal playing time during the initial four matches, he started (and performed well) in the final, a 4–0 success against <a href="/wiki/England_national_under-21_football_team" title="England national under-21 football team">England</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>He made his <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">senior team</a> debut in a <a href="/wiki/Exhibition_game#Association_football" title="Exhibition game">friendly</a> against <a href="/wiki/Malta_national_football_team" title="Malta national football team">Malta</a> on 13 May 2010 in <a href="/wiki/Aachen" title="Aachen">Aachen</a>. He came on as a 46th-minute substitute for <a href="/wiki/Serdar_Tasci" title="Serdar Tasci">Serdar Tasci</a>, taking part in a 3–0 win at <a href="/wiki/New_Tivoli" title="New Tivoli">New Tivoli</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Ramos_quits_Sevilla_to_join_Spurs_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ramos_quits_Sevilla_to_join_Spurs-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Hummels was in the starting line-up for Germany's opening <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> and helped them to a 1–0 victory. He subsequently received high praise for his performance. Hummels went on to play all 450 minutes in Germany's Euro campaign, along with teammates <a href="/wiki/Philipp_Lahm" title="Philipp Lahm">Philipp Lahm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sami_Khedira" title="Sami Khedira">Sami Khedira</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bastian_Schweinsteiger" title="Bastian Schweinsteiger">Bastian Schweinsteiger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Holger_Badstuber" title="Holger Badstuber">Holger Badstuber</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Neuer" title="Manuel Neuer">Manuel Neuer</a>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_(24).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_%2824%29.jpg/220px-Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_%2824%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="293" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_%2824%29.jpg/330px-Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_%2824%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_%2824%29.jpg/440px-Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_%2824%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="998" data-file-height="1331" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Messi_in_Germany_and_Argentina_face_off_in_the_final_of_the_World_Cup_2014_-2014-07-13_(24).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Argentina's <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> (front) battles Hummels for the ball during the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2014 FIFA World Cup Final">final</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Hummels scored the second goal in Germany's 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> in their first game of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> on 16 June, heading a corner from <a href="/wiki/Toni_Kroos" title="Toni Kroos">Toni Kroos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> After missing the team's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Round_of_16" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">round of 16</a> match due to illness, Hummels returned to the team for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Quarter-finals" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">quarter-final</a> against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>, where he scored the winning goal in a 1–0 victory at the <a href="/wiki/Est%C3%A1dio_do_Maracan%C3%A3" class="mw-redirect" title="Estádio do Maracanã">Estádio do Maracanã</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 July 2014, Hummels was named on the 10-man shortlist for FIFA's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup#Golden_Ball" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">Golden Ball</a> award for the tournament's best player.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 10 November 2017, Hummels <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captained</a> Germany for the first time in a 0–0 draw with <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 4 June 2018, Hummels was named in Germany's final 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 23 June, Hummels missed the second group stage match of the World Cup due to a minor injury<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> though his side won the match against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a> with a 2–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> He returned to the side for the final group fixture against <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korea</a> on 27 June, but missed several chances from headers after moving up front during the second half in Germany's unsuccessful attempts to score; ultimately they were defeated 2–0 and eliminated from the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 5 March 2019, national team coach <a href="/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Löw">Joachim Löw</a> confirmed that he would plan without Hummels for the foreseeable future, along with his club teammates <a href="/wiki/J%C3%A9r%C3%B4me_Boateng" title="Jérôme Boateng">Jérôme Boateng</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thomas_M%C3%BCller" title="Thomas Müller">Thomas Müller</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Regarded as one of the best <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)" title="Defender (association football)">defenders</a> in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-theguardian.com_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theguardian.com-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Hummels is a large, consistent, and physically strong player, known for his powerful tackling and strength in the air, as well as his ability to read the game and intercept loose balls.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> A technically gifted and tactically versatile <a href="/wiki/Centre_back" class="mw-redirect" title="Centre back">centre back</a>, he is also capable of playing as a <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-theguardian.com_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theguardian.com-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> his composure, elegance, ball playing ability, and confidence in possession have led him to be compared to compatriot <a href="/wiki/Franz_Beckenbauer" title="Franz Beckenbauer">Franz Beckenbauer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Hummels was born in <a href="/wiki/Bergisch_Gladbach" title="Bergisch Gladbach">Bergisch Gladbach</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Rhine-Westphalia" title="North Rhine-Westphalia">North Rhine-Westphalia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> His father, <a href="/wiki/Hermann_Hummels" title="Hermann Hummels">Hermann Hummels</a>, was a professional footballer and manager. His mother, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Ulla_Holthoff&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ulla Holthoff (page does not exist)">Ulla Holthoff</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;&#91;<a href="https://de.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ulla_Holthoff" class="extiw" title="de:Ulla Holthoff">de</a>&#93;</span>, was a professional water polo player.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> His father worked as youth coordinator at <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> until he was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Stephan_Beckenbauer" title="Stephan Beckenbauer">Stephan Beckenbauer</a>, the son of <a href="/wiki/Franz_Beckenbauer" title="Franz Beckenbauer">Franz Beckenbauer</a>, on 30 March 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> His younger brother <a href="/wiki/Jonas_Hummels" title="Jonas Hummels">Jonas</a> is also a footballer, but had to retire due to injuries.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>His wife, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Cathy_Fischer&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Cathy Fischer (page does not exist)">Cathy Fischer</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&#160;&#91;<a href="https://de.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cathy_Hummels" class="extiw" title="de:Cathy Hummels">de</a>&#93;</span>, was named as Germany's <a href="/wiki/WAGs" title="WAGs">WAG</a> of the year for 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Fischer and Hummels married in June 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> The couple have a son, born on 11 January 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August 2017, he joined the <a href="/wiki/Common_Goal_(charity)" title="Common Goal (charity)">Common Goal Project</a> (an initiative of <a href="/wiki/Juan_Mata" title="Juan Mata">Juan Mata</a>), being the second footballer to donate 1% of his salary to a collective fund that will support football organizations as a tool to generate sustainable social development throughout the world.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mats_Hummels&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>Borussia Dortmund</b><sup id="cite_ref-Soccerway_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Soccerway-79">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
